# J. K. Rowling - Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows Concept Map - Concept Map

Concept map generated from: J. K. Rowling - Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows

**Total Concepts (Nodes):** 898
**Total Relations (Edges):** 1053

## Concepts

### Level 0 - Foundational

#### Grawp

Grawp is an undersized giant, smaller and less mature than typical giants, known in the context as a character distinct from ordinary giants.

**Also known as:** Undersized giant

**Tags:** characters, giants, battle, Harry Potter lore, Giant, wizarding creatures, Fantasy Characters, Harry Potter Universe

**Related:** Centaurs

---

#### The Silencing Charm

A spell cast to silence individuals or crowds by preventing speech or sound.

**Also known as:** Muffliato, Silencio (commonly)

**Tags:** spells, crowd control

**Related:** Dark Arts (shops and influences), Muffliato Spell, Whisper, Silence (in conversation)

---

#### Neville Longbottom

A brave Hogwarts student and son of Aurors, known for his defiance against Voldemort and playing a key role in the Battle of Hogwarts.

**Tags:** characters, heroism, battle

**Related:** Battle of Hogwarts

---

#### Expelliarmus

A disarming spell in the wizarding world that forces an opponent to release whatever they are holding, often used by Harry Potter as his signature move.

**Also known as:** Disarming Charm

**Tags:** spells, defense, magic spells, combat magic, magic, combat, Wizarding, spell, Harry Potter universe, Harry Potter lore

**Related:** Stunning Spell, Wand Allegiance, Harry Potter

---

#### Avada Kedavra

A very powerful and deadly curse in the wizarding world that causes instant death to the victim, classified as one of the Unforgivable Curses.

**Also known as:** Killing Curse

**Tags:** spells, dark magic, unforgivable curses, Harry Potter lore, magic, dark arts, spell, Harry Potter universe

**Related:** Dark Magic

---

#### Wand Allegiance

Wand allegiance is the magical loyalty of a wand to its owner, which can shift if a wand is won from its previous owner by another witch or wizard.

**Also known as:** Wand Mastery, Wand Loyalty

**Tags:** magic theory, wands, Magic, Wizardry, Wandlore

**Related:** The Elder Wand, Expelliarmus, Wands

---

#### The Elder Wand

The Elder Wand, also known as the Deathstick or Wand of Destiny, is a legendary and immensely powerful wand that changes ownership through conquest, often by murder.

**Also known as:** Deathly Hallow wand, Deathstick, Wand of Destiny

**Tags:** magical artifacts, wands, deathly hallows, magic, wandlore, legendary wands

**Related:** Wand Allegiance, Wands

---

#### Centaurs

Magical creatures with the upper body of a human and the lower body of a horse, known for their knowledge of the forest and archery skills.

**Tags:** creatures, magical beings, forest

**Related:** Sylvan Forest Setting, Grawp

---

#### Dementors

Dark, soulless creatures that glide through the forest and cause feelings of cold and despair; they feed on human happiness and are dangerous to wizards.

**Tags:** creatures, dark magic, magical creatures, magic creatures, dark arts, fiction, creature, Wizarding World, Harry Potter universe

**Related:** Patronus, Sylvan Forest Setting

---

#### Nagini

Nagini is a large magical snake associated with Voldemort, often protected by magical enchantments and playing a key role in his power.

**Also known as:** Voldemort's snake, The snake, Nagini the snake

**Tags:** characters, dark magic, Horcrux, Harry Potter Universe, Magical Creatures, Horcruxes, magical creature, Harry Potter lore, dark creatures, Harry Potter, magic creature, fictional character, Dark Arts, Symbolism

**Related:** Horcrux, Snake (Nagini)

---

#### Invisibility Cloak

A magical cloak that renders the wearer invisible, notable for its perfect and infallible concealment, and considered one of the Deathly Hallows.

**Also known as:** Cloak of Invisibility, Cloak, Harry's Cloak

**Tags:** magical artifacts, stealth, magical object, Harry Potter universe, defense, magical artifact, invisibility, protection, magical item, magic, Harry Potter lore, magical items, magical objects, wizardry, Deathly Hallows, magic item, Artifacts, Wizarding World, Artifact, Harry Potter, cloaking, Stealth Magic

**Related:** Battle of Hogwarts

---

#### Shield Charm

A defensive spell cast to protect oneself or others from physical or magical attacks.

**Also known as:** Protego

**Tags:** spells, defense, defensive magic, protection spell

---

#### Horcrux

A Horcrux is a dark magical object in which a dark wizard or witch has hidden a fragment of their soul to attain immortality. Destruction of all Horcruxes is necessary to defeat the creator.

**Also known as:** Soul fragment container, Dark magical object, Dark Horcrux, Dark magical heirloom

**Tags:** dark magic, immortality, magical objects, magic, Harry Potter, artifacts, fiction, Harry Potter universe, magic objects, Dark Arts, Harry Potter lore, Wizardry, magical object, objects, soul, Magical Artifacts, Soul Magic, magic artifact, object, fantasy, Wizarding World

**Related:** Nagini, Locket, Piercing Blue Eye

---

#### Silver Sword with Ruby Handle

A magical weapon capable of killing Horcruxes, such as Nagini, that glows or gleams when used against dark creatures.

**Also known as:** Neville's Sword

**Tags:** magical weapons, Horcrux destruction

**Related:** Sorting Hat

---

#### Sorting Hat

An enchanted hat at Hogwarts that sorts new students into one of the four houses based on their traits, and can present certain artifacts such as the Sword of Gryffindor to worthy individuals.

**Also known as:** The Hat

**Tags:** magic artifacts, Hogwarts, sorting, school tradition, magical artifact, fantasy, magical object, wizarding tradition, Harry Potter lore

**Related:** Silver Sword with Ruby Handle

---

#### Death Eaters

Death Eaters are followers of Voldemort who engage in dark magic, terrorism, and political subversion within the Wizarding World, often using violence and intimidation to achieve their goals.

**Also known as:** Voldemort's followers, Dark Wizards, Death Eater Followers, Dark Lord's Followers

**Tags:** characters, dark magic, antagonists, magic, Harry Potter, faction, group, Harry Potter universe, Dark Wizards, Harry Potter lore, literature, organization, villains, magical factions, dark forces, antagonist faction, wizarding war, dark arts, character group, political group, fantasy, fiction,  antagonists, Wizarding World

**Related:** Daily Prophet, Igor Karkaroff, Pius Thicknesse, Fenrir Greyback, Carrows, Dark Mark, Cloak and Corridor Duel

---

#### Feigned Death

The deliberate action of pretending to be dead to deceive others, often used as a strategy to avoid harm or gain an advantage.

**Also known as:** Feigning Death, Playing Dead

**Tags:** defense strategy, stealth, magic

---

#### Snake (Nagini)

Voldemort's pet snake and a Horcrux, representing a critical target for Harry and his friends in their mission to defeat Voldemort.

**Also known as:** Nagini

**Tags:** magical creature, Horcrux, Harry Potter

**Related:** Nagini

#### Carrows

Dark witch and wizard siblings who served as Death Eater instructors at Hogwarts, likely teaching cruel curses and dark magic such as Fiendfyre to students like Crabbe.

**Tags:** characters, dark magic, Harry Potter, villains, dark arts

**Related:** Death Eaters

---

#### Aragog

A giant spider in the Forbidden Forest, ancestor to many other spiders; its descendants are hostile and can attack Hogwarts when provoked.

**Tags:** magical creature, Harry Potter, Forbidden Forest

**Related:** Hogwarts, Hatred of Spiders

#### Headless Hunt

A cavalcade of ghostly riders in the Harry Potter universe who are known for their headless appearances and nocturnal activities.

**Tags:** magical creature, ghosts, Harry Potter

**Related:** Ghosts of Hogwarts

#### Legilimency

The magical ability to read another person's thoughts or memories, often used to access minds and gain secret information.

#### Voldemort's Scar

A magical mark on Harry Potter's forehead that burns to signal Voldemort's emotions and thoughts, reflecting a magical connection between them.

**Also known as:** Harry's Scar

**Tags:** magic, Harry Potter, connection

**Related:** Legilimency, Voldemort, Lightning Scar

#### Broomstick

A magical flying object used by witches and wizards for transportation and combat during magical battles.

#### Stunning Spell

A magical spell causing unconsciousness or incapacitation, used to subdue opponents without permanent harm in wizard dueling.

#### Battle of Hogwarts

The Battle of Hogwarts is the final conflict between Voldemort’s forces and the defenders of Hogwarts, involving magical combat and the quest to destroy Horcruxes.

**Tags:** event, Harry Potter, magic, history, Events, Harry Potter lore, Conflict

**Related:** Neville Longbottom, Broomstick, Invisibility Cloak

#### Killing Curse

A deadly spell (Avada Kedavra) that causes instant death to its target and played a pivotal role in the creation of the soul fragment inside Harry.

**Also known as:** Avada Kedavra, Killing Curse

**Tags:** magic, dark magic, curse, Harry Potter, Spells, Wizarding World, Harry Potter lore, Harry Potter universe

**Related:** Imperius Curse, Horcrux Destruction

---

#### Room of Requirement

A magical room in Hogwarts Castle that appears only when a person is in great need of it and transforms into whatever the seeker requires at that moment.

**Also known as:** Come and Go Room, Room of Hidden Things

**Tags:** magic, Harry Potter, Hogwarts, magical locations, fiction, location, Hogwarts Locations, Harry Potter lore

**Related:** Ravenclaw Diadem, Hammock (in Room of Requirement), Crystal chandelier

---

#### Fiendfyre

A magical cursed fire in the Harry Potter universe that is sentient, incredibly destructive, capable of mutating into fiery beasts, and able to destroy Horcruxes.

**Also known as:** Cursed Fire

**Tags:** magic, curse, fire, Harry Potter

**Related:** Horcrux Destruction

#### Helena Ravenclaw

The daughter of Rowena Ravenclaw and the ghost known as the Gray Lady, associated with the lost diadem.

**Also known as:** Gray Lady

#### Voldemort

Voldemort is a powerful dark wizard and the primary antagonist who seeks to eliminate Harry Potter and seize control. He is often referred to by names such as 'He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named' and 'You-Know-Who' to avoid speaking his name.

**Also known as:** Tom Riddle, He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named, You-Know-Who, Dark Lord, Lord Voldemort

Magical plants used defensively at Hogwarts; Devil’s Snare entangles intruders, and other plants like Tentacula and Snargaluff pods may be used to fight Death Eaters.

#### Patronus

A Patronus is a magical, positive manifestation conjured by a wizard to repel Dementors, often taking the form of an animal representing the caster's innermost positive feelings.

**Also known as:** Patronus Charm, Patronus Charm Manifestation

**Tags:** magic spell, protection, Harry Potter universe, magic, defense spell, spell, wizardry, defense, Protective Spells, Magic Spells, Protective Magic, Harry Potter Lore, Defensive Magic, communication

**Related:** Dementors, Tonks’ Patronus, Phoenix Patronus

---

#### Apparition

A magical method of instantaneous travel by disappearing from one location and appearing in another; typically used by wizards but house-elves can Apparate inside places like Hogwarts where wizards cannot.

**Also known as:** Apparating, Teleportation, Apparate

**Tags:** magical transportation, Harry Potter universe, Harry Potter lore, magic, transportation, teleportation, spell, Transportation Spell

**Related:** Floo Network, Disapparate

---

#### Floo Network

A magical transportation system enabling witches and wizards to travel instantly between fireplaces linked to the Floo Network by traveling through floo powder and fireplaces.

**Tags:** magical transportation, Harry Potter universe, wizarding world, travel, Magic, Transportation System

**Related:** Apparition, Dark Arts (shops and influences)

#### Imperio

One of the three Unforgivable Curses in wizardry that allows the caster to control another person's actions completely.

**Also known as:** Imperius Curse

**Tags:** magic spell, dark magic, Harry Potter universe

**Related:** Unforgivable Curses

Objects that have disappeared magically, with the concept addressing philosophical or magical questions about their destination, often answered as 'non-being'.

#### Ravenclaw's Diadem

A magical crown owned by Rowena Ravenclaw said to enhance the wisdom of its wearer, later revealed to be a Horcrux hidden within Hogwarts.

#### Lightning Scar

A distinctive scar on Harry Potter's forehead shaped like a lightning bolt that is linked to his connection with Voldemort and reacts when Voldemort is nearby or active.

**Also known as:** Harry's scar, Scar

**Tags:** character traits, magic, symbiosis, Harry Potter, magical artifacts

**Related:** Voldemort's scream of fury, Voldemort's Scar

---

#### Gamp's Law of Elemental Transfiguration

A fundamental magical law stating there are five exceptions to what can be produced or transfigured, one of which is food, meaning food cannot be conjured out of nothing.

**Also known as:** Gamp's Law

**Tags:** magic theory, transfiguration

**Related:** Vanished Objects, Dark Arts (shops and influences)

### Level 2 - Intermediate

#### Horcrux Destruction

The process of destroying a Horcrux by using substances or methods so destructive (such as basilisk venom) that the Horcrux cannot magically repair itself, thereby destroying the soul fragment.

**Prerequisites:** Horcrux Quest

### Level 3 - Advanced

#### Diadem of Ravenclaw

A magical heirloom belonging to Rowena Ravenclaw reputed to enhance the wisdom of its wearer, believed lost for centuries but significant because it is a Horcrux.

**Also known as:** Ravenclaw's Diadem, Ravenclaw’s Diadem

#### Bond between Harry and Voldemort

A unique magical link formed by Voldemort’s unintended Horcrux in Harry and Voldemort’s use of Harry’s blood to regain a body, creating a two-fold connection affecting their wands and destinies.

**Also known as:** Harry-Voldemort Magical Connection

**Tags:** magic, bond, character relationship, dark magic
